If just skip the filter, the codes after the loop will be called with\n693:     // wrong data. For encodeData, the response_encoder->encode() will be called.\n694:     if ((*entry)->end_stream_) {\n695:       return;\n696:     }\n697:     ASSERT(!(state_.filter_call_state_ &
